cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.16.0 FATAL_ERROR)

set(CMAKE_SYSTEM_VERSION 10.0.22000.0 CACHE STRING "" FORCE)
#set(CMAKE_C_STANDARD 99)

project(alfacad C CXX)



################################################################################
## Set target arch type if empty. Visual studio solution generator provides it.
################################################################################
if(NOT CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME)
    set(CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME "x64")
endif()
message("${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME} architecture in use")

if(NOT ("${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}" STREQUAL "Win32"
     OR "${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}" STREQUAL "x64"
     OR "${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}" STREQUAL "x86"))
    message(FATAL_ERROR "${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME} arch is not supported!")
endif()

################################################################################
# Nuget packages function stub.
################################################################################
function(use_package TARGET PACKAGE VERSION)
    message(WARNING "No implementation of use_package. Create yours. "
                    "Package \"${PACKAGE}\" with version \"${VERSION}\" "
                    "for target \"${TARGET}\" is ignored!")
endfunction()

if (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCAD)
#elseif ($<CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE:Release>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Release")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCAD)
#elseif($<CONFIG:Release_PL>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Release_PL")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCADPL)
#elseif($<CONFIG:Release_UA>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Release_UA")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCADUA)
#elseif($<CONFIG:Release_ES>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Release_ES")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCADES)
#elseif ($<CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE:Debug_PL>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug_PL")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCADPL)
    #elseif($<CONFIG:Debug_UA>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug_UA")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCADUA)
    #elseif($<CONFIG:Debug_ES>)
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug_ES")
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCADES)
else()
    set(PROJECT_NAME AlfaCAD)
endif()


if (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug")
    add_compile_definitions("ENGLISH")
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug_PL")
    set(CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE "Debug")
#add_compile_options("$<$<CONFIG:Debug>:-Og>")
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug_UA")
    set(CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE "Debug")
    add_compile_definitions("ENGLISH")
    add_compile_definitions("UKRAINIAN")
#add_compile_options("$<$<CONFIG:Debug>:-Og>")
elseif (CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE STREQUAL "Debug_ES")
    set(CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE "Debug")
    add_compile_definitions("ENGLISH")
    add_compile_definitions("SPANISH")
#add_compile_options("$<$<CONFIG:Debug>:-Og>")
endif()

            MultiThreadedDebugDLL
        >

            MultiThreadedDebugDLL
        >
        $<$<CONFIG:Debug_ES>:
            MultiThreadedDebugDLL
        >
        $<$<CONFIG:Debug>:

        >

            MultiThreadedDLL
        >
        $<$<CONFIG:RelWithDebInfo>:
            MultiThreadedDLL
        >
        $<$<NOT:$<OR:$<CONFIG:Debug_PL>,$<CONFIG:Debug_UA>,$<CONFIG:Debug_ES>,$<CONFIG:Debug>,$<CONFIG:Release_PL>,$<CONFIG:Release_UA>,$<CONFIG:Release_ES>,$<CONFIG:Release>,$<CONFIG:RelWithDebInfo>>>>:${MSVC_RUNTIME_LIBRARY_DEFAULT}>
    )

if(MSVC)
    if("${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}" STREQUAL "Win32")
        target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug_PL>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /ZI
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug_UA>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /ZI
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug_ES>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /ZI
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /ZI
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Release_PL>:
                /Od;
                /Ob1;
                /GF;
                /Gy;
                ${DEFAULT_CXX_DEBUG_INFORMATION_FORMAT}
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Release_UA>:
                /Od;
                /Ob1;
                /GF;
                /Gy;
                ${DEFAULT_CXX_DEBUG_INFORMATION_FORMAT}
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Release_ES>:
                /Od;
                /Ob1;
                /GF;
                /Gy;
                ${DEFAULT_CXX_DEBUG_INFORMATION_FORMAT}
                >
            $<$<CONFIG:Release>:
                /Od;
                /Ob1;
                /GF;
                /Gy;
                ${DEFAULT_CXX_DEBUG_INFORMATION_FORMAT}
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:RelWithDebInfo>:
                /Od;
                /Ob1;
                /GF;
                /Gy;
                ${DEFAULT_CXX_DEBUG_INFORMATION_FORMAT}
            >
            /W3;
            ${DEFAULT_CXX_EXCEPTION_HANDLING};
            /Y-
        )
    elseif("${CMAKE_VS_PLATFORM_NAME}" STREQUAL "x64")
        target_compile_options(${PROJECT_NAME} PRIVATE
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug_PL>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /Zi
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug_UA>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /Zi
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug_ES>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /Zi
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Debug>:
                /Od;
                /RTC1;
                /Zi
            >
            $<$<CONFIG:Release_PL>:
                /Od;
                ${DEFAULT_CXX_DEBUG_INFORMATION_FORMAT}
            >
